                                $(function(){

                                        var tabName = $(this).attr('data-tabName');

                                    });

                                        $(this).addClass('open');

                                        $(this).removeClass('open');
                                    });

                                        activateCallback: activateSubmenu,

                                        activationDelay:0

    <script type="text/javascript">
        $(function(){
            $(".navbarCollapseButton").click(function (e) {
                if($(e.currentTarget).attr('data-target') == '#bs-example-navbar-collapse-2'){
                    $('#collapseSearchbox').removeClass('in');
                    $( "div[data-target='#collapseSearchbox']").addClass('collapsed');
                }else if($(e.currentTarget).attr('data-target') == '#collapseSearchbox'){
                    $('#bs-example-navbar-collapse-2').removeClass('in');
                    $( "button[data-target='#bs-example-navbar-collapse-2']").addClass('collapsed');
                    //Todo bootstrap collapse take time to show search form
                    setTimeout(function() {
                        if($("#collapseSearchbox").hasClass('in')) {
                            $('#txtSearch').focus();
                        }
                    }, 500);
                }
            });
            $("#requestQuoteTop").click(function(){
                addGoogleAnalytics('submit', 'RequestQuoteFor');
            })
            $("#postBuyRequiLink").click(function(){
                addGoogleAnalytics('clicked', 'RequestQuoteTopPostBuyRequirements');
            })
            $("#requestQuoteLinkMobile").click(function(){
                addGoogleAnalytics('clicked', 'RequestQuoteTopMobile');
            })
            $('.zoDropdownHide').click(function(){
                hideLanguageDropdown();
            })
        });
    </script>

                        $(".zoColorPikerHover").mouseenter(function (event) {
                            event.preventDefault();
                            var color = $(event.currentTarget).data('color');
                            $(event.currentTarget).css({color: color, borderColor: color});
                            return false;
                        });
                        $(".zoColorPikerHover").mouseleave(function (event) {
                            event.preventDefault();
                            $(event.currentTarget).removeAttr("style");
                            return false;
                        });

    <div class="modal fade zoShippingHomePopup"  id="myModal" tabindex="-1" role="dialog" aria-labelledby="myModalLabel" data-keyboard="false">

                <button type="button" id='home-popup-close' class="close" data-dismiss="modal" aria-label="Close"><span class="fa fa-times" aria-hidden="true"></span></button>
                <div class="modal-body">
                    <div class="zoPositionRelative">
                        <img src="//res.cloudinary.com/webstore/image/upload/t_homePagePopup/zoodelImages/upload/homePage/logistics-english.jpg" alt="Shipping">

<script type="text/javascript">
    $(function() {
        $(".costSavingTab").click(function (event) {
            event.preventDefault();
            $('.costSavingTab').removeClass('active');
            $(event.currentTarget).addClass('active');
            console.log("SRC New: "+$(event.currentTarget).attr('image-src'))
            $("#cost-saving-img").attr('src', $(event.currentTarget).attr('image-src'));
        });

        todayYMD= function () {
            var now = new Date();
            return [now.getFullYear(), now.getMonth(), now.getDate()].join("-")
        };

        getHomePagePopupImageObject = function () {
            return [
                {
                    value: "en",
                    homePageShippingPopupImage: "//res.cloudinary.com/webstore/image/upload/v1506511714/zoodelImages/upload/homePage/best-price-english.jpg",
                    url: '/en/request-quote',
                    closeColor: 'white'
                },
                {
                    value: "fa",
                    homePageShippingPopupImage: "//res.cloudinary.com/webstore/image/upload/v1506000459/zoodelImages/upload/homePage/popup-20170921.jpg",
                    url: '/en/request-quote',
                    closeColor: 'white'
                },
                {
                    value: "tr",
                    homePageShippingPopupImage: "//res.cloudinary.com/webstore/image/upload/v1500970896/zoodelImages/upload/homePage/logistics-turkish-v2.jpg",
                    url: 'https://myaccount.zoodel.com/en/logistics',
                    closeColor: 'white'
                },
                {
                    value: "ar",
                    homePageShippingPopupImage: "//res.cloudinary.com/webstore/image/upload/v1506511714/zoodelImages/upload/homePage/best-price-arabic.jpg",
                    url: '/en/request-quote',
                    closeColor: 'white'
                },
                {
                    value: "ru",
                    homePageShippingPopupImage: "//res.cloudinary.com/webstore/image/upload/v1506511714/zoodelImages/upload/homePage/best-price-russia.jpg",
                    url: '/en/request-quote',
                    closeColor: 'white'
                },
                {
                    value: "zh",
                    homePageShippingPopupImage: "//res.cloudinary.com/webstore/image/upload/v1500970894/zoodelImages/upload/homePage/logistics-china-v2.jpg",
                    url: 'https://myaccount.zoodel.com/en/logistics',
                    closeColor: 'white'
                }
            ];
        };

        var homePageShippingPopupImageObject = _.findWhere(getHomePagePopupImageObject(), {value: "en"});
        const url = homePageShippingPopupImageObject.url;
        var lastShown = localStorage.getItem("lastShippingPopupDate");
        if (lastShown == null || lastShown != todayYMD()) {
            $('#home-popup-close').css('color', homePageShippingPopupImageObject.closeColor);
            $('.zoShippingHomePopup').find('img')[0].src = homePageShippingPopupImageObject.homePageShippingPopupImage;
            $('.zoShippingHomePopup').modal();
        }

        $(".zoShippingHomePopup").click(function (event) {
            localStorage.setItem("lastShippingPopupDate", todayYMD());
        });
        //Added event to close popup after page redirection to /tenders page
        $(".zoBtnShippingHomePopup").click(function (event) {
            event.preventDefault();
            window.location.href = url;
            localStorage.setItem("lastShippingPopupDate", todayYMD());
            $('.homePageShippingPopup').modal('hide');
            return false;
        });

        $("#signupStartTradingZoodel").click(function (event) {
            event.preventDefault();
            startLoader();
            showModal('login', "en", {selectedTab : "zoJoinFree"});
            return false;
        });
        store.set('productListDisplayView', 'list')
        store.set('sellerListDisplayView', 'list')
    })
</script>

    <p id="back-top">
        <a href="#top"><span></span></a>
    </p>

    <script type="text/javascript">
        $(function () {
            $("#back-top").hide();

            $(window).scroll(function () {
                if ($(this).scrollTop() > 100) {
                    $('#back-top').fadeIn();
                } else {
                    $('#back-top').fadeOut();
                }
            });

            $('#back-top').click(function(){
                $('body,html').animate({
                    scrollTop: 0
                }, 800);
                return false;
            });
        });
    </script>

<div id="commonModal" class="modal fade" role="dialog" data-backdrop="static" data-keyboard="false">
    <div class="modal-dialog">
    </div>
</div>
<script type="text/javascript">
    $(function() {
        $(document).click(function(event) {
            if ($('.zoCountryLanguageDropdownContent').hasClass('collapse in')) {
                hideLanguageDropdown();
            }
        });
        store.set('language', 'en');
        store.set('isRTL', false);
        $.cookie("language", 'en', {path : '/'});
        var countryIso = 'INT';
        $.cookie("defaultCountryISO", countryIso, {path : '/', domain: getCookieDomain()});
        var getCookieDefaultCountryISOValue = $.cookie("defaultCountryISO");
        var language = store.get('language');
        $('.dropdown-toggle').dropdown(); //data-toggle=dropdown works now. Seller sub menu & Language dropdown will be toggled
        $('.zoLanguageRadioBox div input').on('change', function (event) {
            var lang=$(event.currentTarget)[0].lang;
            if($.cookie("language") != lang) {
                $.cookie("language", lang, {path : '/'});
            }
            if(getCookieDefaultCountryISOValue != countryIso) {
                $.cookie("defaultCountryISO", countryIso, {path : '/', domain: getCookieDomain()});
            }
            if(language==lang) {
                $(".zoodle-menu .dropdown").removeClass("open");
                return false;
            }
            var url = window.location.href;
            if(window.location.pathname.length >= 3) {
                // just replace language param to new changed one and redirect to link
                url = url.replace(window.location.pathname.slice(0, 3), '/'+lang)
            }
            window.location.href = url;
        });

        $("#zoSupportedCountriesDropdown li").click(function(){
            var redirectUrl = $(this).attr('domain-name') + '/' + $(this).attr('country-language');
            window.location.href = redirectUrl;
        });

        $('.headerSearchButton').on('click', function () {
            redirectToSearchPage($(this).parents('.zoOverflowHidden').find('#txtSearch').val(), $(this).parents('#searchFieldsContainer').find("#ddlProduct").val());
        });
        $('.homeSearchButton').on('click', function () {
            redirectToSearchPage($(this).parents('.zoOverflowHidden').find('#txtSearch').val(), $(this).parents('#searchFieldsContainer').find("#ddlProduct").val());
        });
        function redirectToSearchPage(searchValue, pageName){
            if(pageName){
                if(searchValue){
                    /*Ajax call to get searchValue matched class.
                    *if exist then we will redirect search byclass
                    * else redirect to search by keyword match
                    */
                    $.get('/' + language + '/getMatchingClass?searchText=' + encodeURIComponent(searchValue) + "&searchType=" + pageName).then(function (responseData) {                 
                        if (responseData) {                          
                            console.log(responseData);
                            window.location.href = '/'+language +'/search/'+ pageName+ '?classId='+responseData;
                        }
                        else{
                            window.location.href = '/'+language +'/search/'+ pageName+'?txtSearch='+encodeURIComponent(searchValue);
                        }
                    });

                } else {
                    window.location.href = '/'+language +'/search/'+pageName;
                }
            }
        }
        $("#afterLoginMenu").hover(function(){
            $(this).addClass('open');
        },function(){
            $(this).removeClass('open');
        });

        $('.headerSearch,.homeSearch').keypress(function (e) {
            if (e.keyCode == 13) {
                redirectToSearchPage($(e.target).val(), $(this).parents('#searchFieldsContainer').find("#ddlProduct").val());
                return false;
            }
        });

        $('.headerSearch,.homeSearch').keyup(function(e){
            var searchParent = $(this).parents('#searchFieldsContainer');
            var searchType = searchParent.find("#ddlProduct").val();
            var searchText = $(e.target).val().trim();

            var isEnter = false;
            if(e.keyCode == 13){
                isEnter = true;
            }

            $(searchParent.find('#seachByUrl')).val('');
            if(searchText.length >= 3){
                $(searchParent.find('#txtSearch')).autocomplete({
                    minLength: 3,
                    source: function (request, response) {
                        $.get('/' + language + '/autosuggestList?searchText=' + encodeURIComponent(searchText) + "&searchType=" + searchType).then(function (responseData) {
                            if (responseData) {
                                response(responseData);
                            }
                        });
                    },

                    focus: function (event, ui) {
                        return false;
                    },

                    select: function (event, ui) {
                        event.preventDefault();
                        if (ui.item) {
                            $(searchParent.find('#txtSearch')).val(ui.item.value);
                            window.location.href = ui.item.url;
                        }
                        return false;
                    },

                    open: function( event, ui ) {
                        if(isEnter){
                            isEnter = false;
                            $(searchParent.find('#txtSearch')).autocomplete('close');
                        }
                        $(".ui-autocomplete li.suggetionCategoryList").last().addClass('lastSuggetionCategoryList');
                        $(".ui-autocomplete li.suggestionClassList").last().addClass('lastSuggetionCategoryList');
                    }

                }).autocomplete( "instance" )._renderItem = function( ul, item ) {
                    /*var itemLabelValue = String(item.label).replace(new RegExp(this.term, "gi"),"<b>$&</b>");*/
                    var itemLabelValue = String(item.label).replace(new RegExp(this.term.replace(/[.*+?^${}()|[\]\\]/g, '\\$&'), "gi"),"<b>$&</b>");

                    var itemClass = '';
                    if (item.showCategory){
                        itemClass = 'suggetionCategoryList';
                    } else {
                        if(!item.isTextSearch) {
                            itemClass = 'suggestionClassList';
                        }
                    }

                    return $("<li></li>")
                            .addClass(itemClass)
                            .data("item.autocomplete", item)
                            .append(itemLabelValue)
                            .appendTo(ul);
                };
            }
        });

        //TODO popup scroll is not working when we use Multiple popup
        $(document).on('hidden.bs.modal','.modal', function () {
            if($('.modal').hasClass('in')) {
                $('body').addClass('modal-open');
            }
        });

        $("body").on('click', "#btnContactSeller,#btnGetLatestPrice", function(event) {
            event.preventDefault();
            startLoader();

            var rfqData = $('#'+$(this).attr('rfqDataId')).attr('rfqData');
            rfqData = JSON.parse(rfqData);

            rfqData['rfqSource'] = 'zoodel-get-latest-price';
            rfqData['rfqHeaderTitle'] = "Get Best Price";

            if ($(event.currentTarget).attr('id') == 'btnContactSeller') {
                addGoogleAnalytics('clicked', 'Contactseller');
                rfqData['rfqSource'] = 'zoodel-product-list';
                rfqData['rfqHeaderTitle'] = "Contact Seller";
            }

            $("#requestQuotePopupContainer").html("");
            $.ajaxSetup({cache:false});
            $.get("/en/request-quote-popup", rfqData, function(response) {
                stopLoader();
                $("#requestQuotePopupContainer").html(response);
                $("#modalRequestQuotePopup").modal();
            });
            return false;
        });
    });
</script>
</body>
</html>
